Uday Kiran cancelled marriage with Chiranjeevi’s daughter? Sister speaks out","abstract":"It has been 12 years since actor Uday Kiran passed away, yet discussions about his professional journey and personal life continue to resurface online. In particular, speculation has persisted for years over why his engagement to Chiranjeevi’s elder daughter, Sushmitha Konidela, was called off. In an earlier interview, Uday’s sister, Sridevi, addressed these rumours. Her remarks from that conversation are once again circulating widely on social media.In the early 2000s, Uday Kiran enjoyed immense popularity in Tollywood, delivering consecutive hits that earned him the title of ‘hat-trick hero’. At the height of his career, he became engaged to Sushmitha. However, in a surprising turn of events, the wedding was cancelled after the engagement. For years, industry gossip suggested that the decision had upset Chiranjeevi and that, as a consequence, Uday allegedly stopped receiving film opportunities.On January 5, 2014, Uday Kiran died by suicide at his residence in Srinagar Colony, Hyderabad. Police investigations at the time indicated that he had been struggling with depression, financial difficulties and a lack of film offers. Sridevi, who resides in Muscat, Oman, later clarified that public assumptions about strained relations between the Mega family and her brother were incorrect. She stated that the decision to call off the wedding was entirely Uday’s. After the engagement, Uday and Sushmitha reportedly had detailed conversations and realised their personalities were incompatible. They mutually agreed to end the engagement, without any external pressure. She firmly denied rumours that Chiranjeevi had taken offence at the cancelled wedding, adding that he continued to extend considerable support to their family during that period.Sridevi also revealed that even before his engagement to Sushmitha, Uday had experienced heartbreak after separating from a woman he deeply loved. The emotional distress reportedly pushed him into depression, and he would often break down. During this difficult phase, she said, Chiranjeevi stood by him as a mentor and guide, encouraging him to move forward in life. Becoming emotional, she remarked, “Chiranjeevi was like a godfather to my brother; he gave a lot of respect to our family.”Sridevi further disclosed that it was Chiranjeevi who had first suggested the idea of the marriage alliance. He reportedly told them that his daughter liked Uday. Believing that marriage and family life might help Uday find stability amid his personal struggles, Chiranjeevi proposed the match. She dismissed allegations that he had any personal motive behind the proposal, describing him as one of the few individuals who genuinely wished well for her brother.Sridevi concluded by emphasising that no one should be held responsible for her brother’s death.
